VERILOG CODE:
// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hours, minutes, seconds;
    reg am_pm;

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = am_pm;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            hours <= 8'h12; // Representing 12
            minutes <= 8'h00;
            seconds <= 8'h00;
            am_pm <= 0; // AM
        end
        else if (ena) begin
            if (seconds == 8'h59) begin
                seconds <= 8'h00;
                if (minutes == 8'h59) begin
                    minutes <= 8'h00;
                    if (hours == 8'h12) begin
                        hours <= 8'h01;
                        am_pm <= ~am_pm; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end
                    else if (hours == 8'h11) begin
                        hours <= 8'h12;
                    end
                    else begin
                        hours <= hours + 1;
                    end
                end
                else begin
                    minutes <= minutes + 1;
                end
            end
            else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 1;
            end
        end
    end

endmodule

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hours, minutes, seconds;
    reg pm_reg;
    
    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = pm_reg;
    
    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            hours <= 8'h12; // 12:00:00
            minutes <= 8'h00;
            seconds <= 8'h00;
            pm_reg <= 1'b0; // AM
        end else if (ena) begin
            if (seconds == 8'h59) begin
                seconds <= 8'h00;
                if (minutes == 8'h59) begin
                    minutes <= 8'h00;
                    if (hours == 8'h12) begin
                        hours <= 8'h01;
                        pm_reg <= ~pm_reg;
                    end else if (hours == 8'h11) begin
                        hours <= 8'h12;
                    end else begin
                        hours <= hours + 1;
                    end
                end else begin
                    minutes <= minutes + 1;
                end
            end else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 1;
            end
        end
    end

endmodule

trimming text with ```verilog
State ends with endmodule
Initiating comile/functionality check.
VERILOG CODE:
// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hours, minutes, seconds;
    reg pm_reg;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset the clock to 12:00:00 AM
            hours <= 8'h12; // BCD for 12
            minutes <= 8'h00;
            seconds <= 8'h00;
            pm_reg <= 0; // AM
        end else if (ena) begin
            // Increment the seconds
            if (seconds == 8'h59) begin
                seconds <= 8'h00;
                // Increment the minutes
                if (minutes == 8'h59) begin
                    minutes <= 8'h00;
                    // Increment the hours
                    if (hours == 8'h12) begin
                        hours <= 8'h01;
                        pm_reg <= ~pm_reg; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end else if (hours == 8'h11) begin
                        hours <= 8'h12;
                    end else begin
                        hours <= hours + 8'h01;
                    end
                end else begin
                    minutes <= minutes + 8'h01;
                end
            end else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 8'h01;
            end
        end
    end

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = pm_reg;

endmodule

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg pm_r;
    reg [7:0] hh_r, mm_r, ss_r;

    assign hh = hh_r;
    assign mm = mm_r;
    assign ss = ss_r;
    assign pm = pm_r;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            hh_r <= 8'b0001_0010; // BCD for 12
            mm_r <= 8'b0000_0000; // BCD for 00
            ss_r <= 8'b0000_0000; // BCD for 00
            pm_r <= 1'b0;         // AM
        end else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (ss_r == 8'b0101_1001) begin // BCD for 59 seconds
                ss_r <= 8'b0000_0000;      // Reset to 00 seconds
                // Increment minutes
                if (mm_r == 8'b0101_1001) begin // BCD for 59 minutes
                    mm_r <= 8'b0000_0000;      // Reset to 00 minutes
                    // Increment hours
                    if (hh_r == 8'b0001_0010) begin // BCD for 12 hours
                        hh_r <= 8'b0000_0001;       // Reset to 01 hour
                        pm_r <= ~pm_r;             // Toggle AM/PM
                    end else if (hh_r == 8'b0001_0001) begin // BCD for 11 hours
                        hh_r <= 8'b0001_0010;              // Advance to 12 hour
                    end else begin
                        hh_r <= hh_r + 1'b1; // Increment hour
                    end
                end else begin
                    mm_r <= mm_r + 1'b1; // Increment minute
                end
            end else begin
                ss_r <= ss_r + 1'b1; // Increment second
            end
        end
    end

endmodule

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hour;
    reg [7:0] minute;
    reg [7:0] second;
    reg pm_reg;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            hour <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12:00:00 AM
            minute <= 8'b0000_0000;
            second <= 8'b0000_0000;
            pm_reg <= 0;
        end 
        else if (ena) begin
            if (second == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 seconds
                second <= 8'b0000_0000; // reset seconds
                if (minute == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 minutes
                    minute <= 8'b0000_0000; // reset minutes
                    if (hour == 8'b0001_0010) begin // 12
                        hour <= 8'b0000_0001; // 1
                        pm_reg <= ~pm_reg; // toggle AM/PM
                    end
                    else if (hour == 8'b0001_0001) begin // 11
                        hour <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12
                    end
                    else begin
                        hour <= hour + 1; // increment hours
                    end
                end 
                else begin
                    minute <= minute + 1; // increment minutes
                end
            end 
            else begin
                second <= second + 1; // increment seconds
            end
        end
    end

    assign hh = hour;
    assign mm = minute;
    assign ss = second;
    assign pm = pm_reg;

endmodule

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

    reg [7:0] minutes;
    reg [7:0] hours;

    assign mm = minutes;
    assign hh = hours;

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg pm_reg;
    reg [7:0] hh_reg, mm_reg, ss_reg;
    
    assign pm = pm_reg;
    assign hh = hh_reg;
    assign mm = mm_reg;
    assign ss = ss_reg;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset to 12:00:00 AM
            hh_reg <= 8'h12; // 12 in BCD
            mm_reg <= 8'h00;
            ss_reg <= 8'h00;
            pm_reg <= 0; // AM
        end else if (ena) begin
            if (ss_reg == 8'h59) begin

VERILOG CODE:
// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg pm_reg;
    reg [7:0] hh_reg;
    reg [7:0] mm_reg;
    reg [7:0] ss_reg;

    assign pm = pm_reg;
    assign hh = hh_reg;
    assign mm = mm_reg;
    assign ss = ss_reg;
    
    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            hh_reg <= 8'h12; // 12:00:00 AM
            mm_reg <= 8'h00;
            ss_reg <= 8'h00;
            pm_reg <= 1'b0;
        end else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (ss_reg == 8'h59) begin
                ss_reg <= 8'h00;
                // Increment minutes
                if (mm_reg == 8'h59) begin
                    mm_reg <= 8'h00;
                    // Increment hours
                    if (hh_reg == 8'h12) begin
                        hh_reg <= 8'h01;
                        pm_reg <= ~pm_reg; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end else if (hh_reg == 8'h11) begin
                        hh_reg <= 8'h12; // 11:XX -> 12:XX
                    end else begin
                        hh_reg <= hh_reg + 1;
                    end
                end else begin
                    mm_reg <= mm_reg + 1;
                end
            end else begin
                ss_reg <= ss_reg + 1;
            end
        end
    end

endmodule

State ends with endmodule
Initiating comile/functionality check.
VERILOG CODE:
// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hours;
    reg [7:0] minutes;
    reg [7:0] seconds;
    reg am_pm;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset the clock to 12:00:00 AM
            hours <= 8'h12;    // "12" in BCD
            minutes <= 8'h00;  // "00" in BCD
            seconds <= 8'h00;  // "00" in BCD
            am_pm <= 0;        // AM
        end else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (seconds == 8'h59) begin
                seconds <= 8'h00;

                // Increment minutes
                if (minutes == 8'h59) begin
                    minutes <= 8'h00;

                    // Increment hours
                    if (hours == 8'h12) begin
                        hours <= 8'h01;
                        am_pm <= ~am_pm;  // Toggle AM/PM
                    end else if (hours == 8'h11) begin
                        hours <= 8'h12;
                    end else begin
                        hours <= hours + 1;
                    end

                end else begin
                    minutes <= minutes + 1;
                end

            end else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 1;
            end
        end
    end

    // Assign outputs
    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = am_pm;

endmodule

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] seconds;
    reg [7:0] minutes;
    reg [7:0] hours;
    reg pm_reg;

    assign ss = seconds;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign hh = hours;
    assign pm = pm_reg;

    always @(posedge clk) begin
        if (reset) begin
            seconds <= 8'h00;
            minutes <= 8'h00;
            hours <= 8'h12;
            pm_reg <= 1'b0;
        end
        else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (seconds[3:0] == 9) begin
                if (seconds[7:4] == 5) begin
                    seconds <= 8'h00; // 59 -> 00
                    // Increment minutes
                    if (minutes[3:0] == 9) begin
                        if (minutes[7:4] == 5) begin
                            minutes <= 8'h00; // 59 -> 00
                            // Increment hours
                            if (hours == 8'h12) begin
                                hours <= 8'h01;
                                pm_reg <= ~pm_reg; // Toggle AM/PM
                            end
                            else if (hours[3:0] == 9) begin
                                if (hours[7:4] == 1) begin
                                    hours <= 8'h10; // 19 -> 20
                                end
                            end
                            else begin
                                hours <= hours + 8'h01;
                            end
                        end
                        else begin
                            minutes <= {minutes[7:4] + 1'b1, 4'h0}; // e.g., 09 -> 10
                        end
                    end
                    else begin
                        minutes <= minutes + 8'h01;
                    end
                end
                else begin
                    seconds <= {seconds[7:4] + 1'b1, 4'h0}; // e.g., 09 -> 10
                end
            end
            else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 8'h01;
            end
        end
    end

endmodule

VERILOG CODE:
// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hours;
    reg [7:0] minutes;
    reg [7:0] seconds;
    reg am_pm;

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = am_pm;

    always @(posedge clk) begin
        if (reset) begin
            hours <= 8'h12;  // 12 in BCD
            minutes <= 8'h00;
            seconds <= 8'h00;
            am_pm <= 0; // AM
        end
        else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (seconds == 8'h59) begin
                seconds <= 8'h00;
                // Increment minutes
                if (minutes == 8'h59) begin
                    minutes <= 8'h00;
                    // Increment hours
                    if (hours == 8'h12) begin
                        hours <= 8'h01;
                        am_pm <= ~am_pm; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end
                    else if (hours == 8'h11) begin
                        hours <= 8'h12; // 11:59 -> 12:00
                    end
                    else begin
                        hours <= hours + 8'h1; // BCD increment
                    end
                end
                else begin
                    minutes <= minutes + 8'h1; // BCD increment
                end
            end
            else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 8'h1; // BCD increment
            end
        end
    end

endmodule

Initiating comile/functionality check.
VERILOG CODE:
// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hours, minutes, seconds; 
    reg pm_flag;

    always @(posedge clk) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset the time to 12:00:00 AM
            hours <= 8'b00010010; // 12 in BCD
            minutes <= 8'b00000000; // 00 in BCD
            seconds <= 8'b00000000; // 00 in BCD
            pm_flag <= 1'b0; // AM
        end else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (seconds == 8'b01011001) begin // 59 in BCD
                seconds <= 8'b00000000; // Reset seconds to 00

                // Increment minutes
                if (minutes == 8'b01011001) begin // 59 in BCD
                    minutes <= 8'b00000000; // Reset minutes to 00

                    // Increment hours
                    if (hours == 8'b00010010) begin // 12 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b00000001; // Set hours to 01
                        pm_flag <= ~pm_flag; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end else if (hours == 8'b00010001) begin // 11 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b00010010; // Set hours to 12
                    end else begin
                        hours <= hours + 1'b1; // Increment hours
                    end
                end else begin
                    minutes <= minutes + 1'b1; // Increment minutes
                end
            end else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 1'b1; // Increment seconds
            end
        end
    end

    // Assigning outputs
    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = pm_flag;
endmodule

VERILOG CODE:
// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] seconds;
    reg [7:0] minutes;
    reg [7:0] hours;
    reg pm_reg;

    assign ss = seconds;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign hh = hours;
    assign pm = pm_reg;

    always @(posedge clk) begin
        if (reset) begin
            hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12
            minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00
            seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00
            pm_reg <= 0; // AM
        end
        else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (seconds == 8'b0101_1001) begin
                seconds <= 8'b0000_0000;

                // Increment minutes
                if (minutes == 8'b0101_1001) begin
                    minutes <= 8'b0000_0000;

                    // Increment hours
                    if (hours == 8'b0001_0010) begin
                        hours <= 8'b0000_0001; // 01
                        pm_reg <= ~pm_reg; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end
                    else if (hours == 8'b0001_0001) begin
                        hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12
                    end
                    else begin
                        hours <= hours + 1;
                    end
                end
                else begin
                    minutes <= minutes + 1;
                end
            end
            else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 1;
            end
        end
    end
endmodule

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hour;
    reg [7:0] minute;
    reg [7:0] second;
    reg pm_reg;
    
    assign hh = hour;
    assign mm = minute;
    assign ss = second;
    assign pm = pm_reg;
    
    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset to 12:00:00 AM
            hour <= 8'b0001_0010;  // 12 in BCD
            minute <= 8'b0000_0000;  // 00 in BCD
            second <= 8'b0000_0000;  // 00 in BCD
            pm_reg <= 1'b0;  // AM

            // Increment seconds

                second <= 8'b0000_0000;
                // Increment minutes
                if (minute == 8'b0101_1001) begin
                    minute <= 8'b0000_0000;
                    // Increment hours
                    if (hour == 8'b0001_0010) begin
                        hour <= 8'b0000_0001;  // Wrap around to 1
                        pm_reg <= ~pm_reg;  // Toggle AM/PM
                    end else if (hour == 8'b0001_0001) begin
                        hour <= 8'b0001_0010;  // 11 to 12
                    end else begin
                        hour <= hour + 1'b1;  // Increment hour
                    end
                end else begin
                    minute <= minute + 1'b1;  // Increment minute
                end
            end else begin
                second <= second + 1'b1;  // Increment second
            end
        end
    end

VERILOG CODE:
// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

    reg pm_reg;
    reg [7:0] hh_reg;
    reg [7:0] mm_reg;
    reg [7:0] ss_reg;

    assign pm = pm_reg;
    assign hh = hh_reg;
    assign mm = mm_reg;
    assign ss = ss_reg;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset to 12:00:00 AM
            hh_reg <= 8'h12;
            mm_reg <= 8'h00;
            ss_reg <= 8'h00;
            pm_reg <= 0;
        end else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (ss_reg == 8'h59) begin
                ss_reg <= 8'h00;

                // Increment minutes
                if (mm_reg == 8'h59) begin
                    mm_reg <= 8'h00;

                    // Increment hours
                    if (hh_reg == 8'h12) begin
                        hh_reg <= 8'h01;
                        pm_reg <= ~pm_reg; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end else if (hh_reg == 8'h11) begin
                        hh_reg <= 8'h12; // Transition from 11 to 12
                    end else begin
                        hh_reg <= hh_reg + 8'h01;
                    end
                end else begin
                    mm_reg <= mm_reg + 8'h01;
                end
            end else begin
                ss_reg <= ss_reg + 8'h01;
            end
        end
    end

endmodule

                    end

                end
            end else begin
                ss_reg <= ss_reg + 8'h01;
            end
        end
    end

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

    reg [7:0] minutes;
    reg [7:0] seconds;

    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;

            seconds <= 0;

                    end

Initiating comile/functionality check.
VERILOG CODE:
// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg pm_reg;
    reg [3:0] sh, sl; // sh: high digit of hour, sl: low digit of hour
    reg [3:0] mh, ml; // mh: high digit of minute, ml: low digit of minute
    reg [3:0] sth, stl; // sth: high digit of second, stl: low digit of second

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset to 12:00:00 AM
            sh <= 4'd1;
            sl <= 4'd2;
            mh <= 4'd0;
            ml <= 4'd0;
            sth <= 4'd0;
            stl <= 4'd0;
            pm_reg <= 1'b0;
        end
        else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (stl == 4'd9) begin
                stl <= 4'd0;
                if (sth == 4'd5) begin
                    sth <= 4'd0;
                    // Increment minutes
                    if (ml == 4'd9) begin
                        ml <= 4'd0;
                        if (mh == 4'd5) begin
                            mh <= 4'd0;
                            // Increment hours
                            if (sl == 4'd9) begin
                                sl <= 4'd0;
                                if (sh == 4'd1) begin
                                    sh <= 4'd0;
                                    pm_reg <= ~pm_reg; // Toggle AM/PM
                                end else begin
                                    sh <= 4'd1;
                                end
                            end else begin
                                sl <= sl + 4'd1;
                                if (sh == 4'd1 && sl == 4'd2) begin
                                    sl <= 4'd1;
                                    sh <= 4'd0;
                                    pm_reg <= ~pm_reg; // Toggle AM/PM
                                end
                            end
                        end else begin
                            mh <= mh + 4'd1;
                        end
                    end else begin
                        ml <= ml + 4'd1;
                    end
                end else begin
                    sth <= sth + 4'd1;
                end
            end else begin
                stl <= stl + 4'd1;
            end
        end
    end

    assign hh = {sh, sl};
    assign mm = {mh, ml};
    assign ss = {sth, stl};
    assign pm = pm_reg;

endmodule

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

Initiating comile/functionality check.
VERILOG CODE:
// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);


    reg am_pm;
    reg [7:0] hours;
    reg [7:0] minutes;
    reg [7:0] seconds;
    
    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset time to 12:00:00 AM
            hours <= 8'h12;
            minutes <= 8'h00;
            seconds <= 8'h00;
            am_pm <= 1'b0; // AM
        end else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (seconds == 8'h59) begin
                seconds <= 8'h00;
                
                // Increment minutes
                if (minutes == 8'h59) begin
                    minutes <= 8'h00;
                    
                    // Increment hours
                    if (hours == 8'h12) begin
                        hours <= 8'h01;
                        am_pm <= ~am_pm; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end else if (hours == 8'h11) begin
                        hours <= 8'h12;
                    end else begin
                        hours <= hours + 1;
                    end
                end else begin
                    minutes <= minutes + 1;
                end
            end else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 1;
            end
        end
    end
    
    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = am_pm;

endmodule

Initiating comile/functionality check.
VERILOG CODE:
// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);


    reg [7:0] hours, minutes, seconds;
    reg pm_reg;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            hours <= 8'b00010010; // 12
            minutes <= 8'b00000000; // 00
            seconds <= 8'b00000000; // 00
            pm_reg <= 0; // AM
        end else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (seconds == 8'b01011001) begin // 59
                seconds <= 8'b00000000;
                
                // Increment minutes
                if (minutes == 8'b01011001) begin // 59
                    minutes <= 8'b00000000;
                    
                    // Increment hours
                    if (hours == 8'b00010010) begin // 12
                        hours <= 8'b00000001; // 01
                        pm_reg <= ~pm_reg; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end else if (hours == 8'b00001001) begin // 09, next is 10
                        hours <= 8'b00010000; // 10
                    end else if (hours == 8'b00011001) begin // 19, next is 20
                        hours <= 8'b00100000; // 20
                    end else if (hours == 8'b00100000) begin // 20, next is 21
                        hours <= 8'b00100001; // 21
                    end else begin
                        hours <= hours + 1;
                    end
                end else begin
                    minutes <= minutes + 1;
                end
            end else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 1;
            end
        end
    end

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = pm_reg;

endmodule

Initiating comile/functionality check.
VERILOG CODE:
// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg pm_reg;
    reg [7:0] hh_reg, mm_reg, ss_reg;
    
    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            hh_reg <= 8'h12; // 12 hours for BCD
            mm_reg <= 8'h00; // 00 minutes for BCD
            ss_reg <= 8'h00; // 00 seconds for BCD
            pm_reg <= 0;     // AM
        end
        else if (ena) begin
            // Seconds Counter
            if (ss_reg == 8'h59) begin
                ss_reg <= 8'h00;
                // Minutes Counter
                if (mm_reg == 8'h59) begin
                    mm_reg <= 8'h00;
                    // Hours Counter
                    if (hh_reg == 8'h12) begin
                        hh_reg <= 8'h01;
                        pm_reg <= ~pm_reg; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end
                    else if (hh_reg == 8'h11) begin
                        hh_reg <= 8'h12;
                    end
                    else begin
                        hh_reg <= hh_reg + 8'h01; // Increment hour
                    end
                end
                else begin
                    mm_reg <= mm_reg + 8'h01; // Increment minute
                end
            end
            else begin
                ss_reg <= ss_reg + 8'h01; // Increment second
            end
        end
    end

    assign hh = hh_reg;
    assign mm = mm_reg;
    assign ss = ss_reg;
    assign pm = pm_reg;

endmodule

Output Verilog module compiles successfully.
Functionality check...

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hh_reg;
    reg [7:0] mm_reg;
    reg [7:0] ss_reg;
    reg pm_reg;

    always @(posedge clk) begin
        if (reset) begin
            hh_reg <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12 in BCD
            mm_reg <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            ss_reg <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            pm_reg <= 1'b0;         // AM
        end
        else if (ena) begin
            if (ss_reg == 8'b0101_1001) begin
                ss_reg <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset seconds to 00
                if (mm_reg == 8'b0101_1001) begin
                    mm_reg <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset minutes to 00
                    if (hh_reg == 8'b0001_0010) begin
                        hh_reg <= 8'b0000_0001; // Roll over from 12 to 01
                        pm_reg <= ~pm_reg;      // Toggle AM/PM
                    end else if (hh_reg == 8'b0000_1001) begin
                        hh_reg <= 8'b0001_0000; // 09 to 10
                    end else begin
                        hh_reg[3:0] <= hh_reg[3:0] + 1;
                    end
                end else if (mm_reg[3:0] == 4'b1001) begin
                    mm_reg[3:0] <= 4'b0000; // Roll over ones place
                    mm_reg[7:4] <= mm_reg[7:4] + 1; // Increment tens place
                end else begin
                    mm_reg[3:0] <= mm_reg[3:0] + 1;
                end
            end else if (ss_reg[3:0] == 4'b1001) begin
                ss_reg[3:0] <= 4'b0000; // Roll over ones place
                ss_reg[7:4] <= ss_reg[7:4] + 1; // Increment tens place
            end else begin
                ss_reg[3:0] <= ss_reg[3:0] + 1;
            end
        end
    end

    assign hh = hh_reg;
    assign mm = mm_reg;
    assign ss = ss_reg;
    assign pm = pm_reg;

endmodule

VERILOG CODE:
// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

    reg [7:0] hour, minute, second;
    reg pm_reg;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset to 12:00:00 AM
            hour <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12 in BCD
            minute <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            second <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            pm_reg <= 1'b0; // AM
        end
        else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (second == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                second <= 8'b0000_0000;
                // Increment minutes
                if (minute == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                    minute <= 8'b0000_0000;
                    // Increment hours
                    if (hour == 8'b0001_0010) begin // 12 in BCD
                        hour <= 8'b0000_0001; // 01 in BCD
                        pm_reg <= ~pm_reg; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end
                    else if (hour == 8'b0001_0001) begin // 11 in BCD
                        hour <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12 in BCD
                    end
                    else begin
                        // General hour increment
                        if (hour[3:0] == 4'b1001) begin
                            hour <= {hour[7:4] + 1'b1, 4'b0000};
                        end else begin
                            hour <= hour + 1'b1;
                        end
                    end
                end
                else begin
                    // General minute increment
                    if (minute[3:0] == 4'b1001) begin
                        minute <= {minute[7:4] + 1'b1, 4'b0000};
                    end else begin
                        minute <= minute + 1'b1;
                    end
                end
            end
            else begin
                // General second increment
                if (second[3:0] == 4'b1001) begin
                    second <= {second[7:4] + 1'b1, 4'b0000};
                end else begin
                    second <= second + 1'b1;
                end
            end
        end
    end

    // Outputs
    assign hh = hour;
    assign mm = minute;
    assign ss = second;
    assign pm = pm_reg;

endmodule

VERILOG CODE:
// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hours, minutes, seconds;
    reg pm_reg;

    // Assign outputs
    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = pm_reg;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            hours <= 8'h12; // 12:00
            minutes <= 8'h00;
            seconds <= 8'h00;
            pm_reg <= 0;    // AM
        end
        else if (ena) begin
            if (seconds == 8'h59) begin
                seconds <= 8'h00;
                if (minutes == 8'h59) begin
                    minutes <= 8'h00;
                    if (hours == 8'h12) begin
                        hours <= 8'h01;
                        pm_reg <= ~pm_reg; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end
                    else if (hours == 8'h11) begin
                        hours <= 8'h12;
                    end
                    else begin
                        hours <= hours + 8'h01;
                    end
                end
                else begin
                    minutes <= minutes + 8'h01;
                end
            end
            else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 8'h01;
            end
        end
    end

endmodule

Initiating comile/functionality check.
VERILOG CODE:
// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);


    reg [7:0] hh_reg, mm_reg, ss_reg;
    reg pm_reg;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset the clock to 12:00:00 AM
            hh_reg <= 8'h12; // 12 in BCD
            mm_reg <= 8'h00; // 00 in BCD
            ss_reg <= 8'h00; // 00 in BCD
            pm_reg <= 1'b0; // AM
        end
        else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (ss_reg == 8'h59) begin
                ss_reg <= 8'h00;

                // Increment minutes
                if (mm_reg == 8'h59) begin
                    mm_reg <= 8'h00;

                    // Increment hours
                    if (hh_reg == 8'h12) begin
                        hh_reg <= 8'h01;
                        pm_reg <= ~pm_reg; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end
                    else if (hh_reg == 8'h11) begin
                        hh_reg <= 8'h12; // Advance from 11 to 12
                    end
                    else begin
                        hh_reg <= hh_reg + 1'b1;
                    end
                end
                else begin
                    mm_reg <= mm_reg + 1'b1;
                end
            end
            else begin
                ss_reg <= ss_reg + 1'b1;
            end
        end
    end

    assign hh = hh_reg;
    assign mm = mm_reg;
    assign ss = ss_reg;
    assign pm = pm_reg;

endmodule
Compilation check...
Output Verilog module compiles successfully.
Functionality check...

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hour, minute, second;
    reg pm_reg;

    assign hh = hour;
    assign mm = minute;
    assign ss = second;
    assign pm = pm_reg;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            hour <= 8'b0001_0010;  // 12
            minute <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00
            second <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00
            pm_reg <= 1'b0;         // AM
        end else if (ena) begin
            if (second == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59
                second <= 8'b0000_0000;       // Reset to 00
                if (minute == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59
                    minute <= 8'b0000_0000;   // Reset to 00
                    if (hour == 8'b0001_0010) begin // 12
                        hour <= 8'b0000_0001;  // Reset to 1
                        pm_reg <= ~pm_reg;     // Toggle AM/PM
                    end else if (hour == 8'b0001_0001) begin // 11
                        hour <= 8'b0001_0010;  // Advance to 12
                    end else begin
                        hour[3:0] <= hour[3:0] + 1'b1;
                    end
                end else if (minute[3:0] == 4'b1001) begin
                    minute[3:0] <= 4'b0000;
                    minute[7:4] <= minute[7:4] + 1'b1;
                end else begin
                    minute[3:0] <= minute[3:0] + 1'b1;
                end
            end else if (second[3:0] == 4'b1001) begin
                second[3:0] <= 4'b0000;
                second[7:4] <= second[7:4] + 1'b1;
            end else begin
                second[3:0] <= second[3:0] + 1'b1;
            end
        end
    end

endmodule

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);


    reg [7:0] hours;
    reg [7:0] minutes;
    reg [7:0] seconds;
    reg pm_reg;

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = pm_reg;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Resetting all counters and the PM indicator
            hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12
            minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00
            seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00
            pm_reg <= 0; // AM
        end else if (ena) begin
            // Increment the seconds
            if (seconds == 8'b0101_1001) begin
                seconds <= 8'b0000_0000;
                
                // Increment the minutes
                if (minutes == 8'b0101_1001) begin
                    minutes <= 8'b0000_0000;
                    
                    // Increment the hours
                    if (hours == 8'b0001_0010) begin
                        hours <= 8'b0000_0001; // 12 -> 01
                        pm_reg <= ~pm_reg; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end else if (hours == 8'b0001_0001) begin
                        hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // 11 -> 12
                    end else begin
                        hours <= hours + 1; // General case
                    end
                end else begin
                    minutes <= minutes + 1;
                end
            end else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 1;
            end
        end
    end

endmodule

Output Verilog module compiles successfully.

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

    reg [7:0] hh_reg, mm_reg, ss_reg;
    reg pm_reg;

    assign hh = hh_reg;
    assign mm = mm_reg;
    assign ss = ss_reg;
    assign pm = pm_reg;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset to 12:00:00 AM
            hh_reg <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12 in BCD
            mm_reg <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            ss_reg <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            pm_reg <= 0; // AM
        end else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (ss_reg == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59
                ss_reg <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset seconds to 00
                
                // Increment minutes
                if (mm_reg == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59
                    mm_reg <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset minutes to 00
                    
                    // Increment hours
                    if (hh_reg == 8'b0001_0010) begin // 12
                        hh_reg <= 8'b0000_0001; // 1 in BCD
                        pm_reg <= ~pm_reg; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end else if (hh_reg == 8'b0001_0001) begin // 11
                        hh_reg <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12 in BCD
                    end else begin
                        hh_reg <= hh_reg + 1; // Increment hour
                    end
                end else begin
                    mm_reg <= mm_reg + ((mm_reg[3:0] == 4'b1001) ? 4'b0110 : 4'b0001); // Increment BCD minutes
                end
            end else begin
                ss_reg <= ss_reg + ((ss_reg[3:0] == 4'b1001) ? 4'b0110 : 4'b0001); // Increment BCD seconds
            end
        end
    end
endmodule

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);


    reg [7:0] hours;
    reg [7:0] minutes;
    reg [7:0] seconds;
    reg am_pm;

    always @(posedge clk) begin
        if (reset) begin
            hours <= 8'b0001_0010;  // 12 in BCD
            minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            am_pm <= 1'b0; // 0 for AM
        end else if (ena) begin
            if (seconds == 8'b0101_1001) begin  // 59 in BCD
                seconds <= 8'b0000_0000;
                if (minutes == 8'b0101_1001) begin  // 59 in BCD
                    minutes <= 8'b0000_0000;
                    if (hours == 8'b0001_0010) begin  // 12 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0000_0001;  // 1 in BCD
                        am_pm <= ~am_pm;  // Toggle AM/PM
                    end else if (hours == 8'b0000_1001) begin  // 9 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0001_0000;  // 10 in BCD
                    end else if (hours == 8'b0001_0000) begin  // 10 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0001_0001;  // 11 in BCD
                    end else if (hours == 8'b0001_0001) begin  // 11 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0001_0010;  // 12 in BCD
                    end else begin
                        hours <= hours + 8'b0000_0001;  // Increment hours
                    end
                end else begin
                    if (minutes[3:0] == 4'b1001) begin
                        minutes <= {minutes[7:4] + 4'b0001, 4'b0000};  // Increment tens digit of minutes
                    end else begin
                        minutes <= minutes + 8'b0000_0001;  // Increment minutes
                    end
                end
            end else begin
                if (seconds[3:0] == 4'b1001) begin
                    seconds <= {seconds[7:4] + 4'b0001, 4'b0000};  // Increment tens digit of seconds
                end else begin
                    seconds <= seconds + 8'b0000_0001;  // Increment seconds
                end
            end
        end
    end

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = am_pm;

endmodule

Initiating comile/functionality check.
VERILOG CODE:
// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hh_reg, mm_reg, ss_reg;
    reg pm_reg;

    // Assign outputs
    assign hh = hh_reg;
    assign mm = mm_reg;
    assign ss = ss_reg;
    assign pm = pm_reg;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset to 12:00:00 AM
            hh_reg <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12
            mm_reg <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00
            ss_reg <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00
            pm_reg <= 1'b0;         // AM
        end else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (ss_reg == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59
                ss_reg <= 8'b0000_0000; // roll over to 00
                // Increment minutes
                if (mm_reg == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59
                    mm_reg <= 8'b0000_0000; // roll over to 00
                    // Increment hours
                    if (hh_reg == 8'b0001_0010) begin // 12
                        hh_reg <= 8'b0000_0001; // roll over to 01
                        pm_reg <= ~pm_reg;     // toggle AM/PM
                    end else if (hh_reg == 8'b0001_0001) begin // 11
                        hh_reg <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12
                    end else begin
                        hh_reg <= hh_reg + 1'b1;
                    end
                end else begin
                    mm_reg <= mm_reg + 1'b1;
                end
            end else begin
                ss_reg <= ss_reg + 1'b1;
            end
        end
    end

endmodule

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hours;
    reg [7:0] mins;
    reg [7:0] secs;
    reg is_pm;

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = mins;
    assign ss = secs;
    assign pm = is_pm;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            hours <= 8'h12; // 12:00:00 AM
            mins <= 8'h00;
            secs <= 8'h00;
            is_pm <= 1'b0;  // AM
        end

                secs <= 8'h00;
                // Increment minutes
                if (mins == 8'h59) begin
                    mins <= 8'h00;

                        is_pm <= ~is_pm; // Toggle AM/PM

                    end
                end

                    mins <= mins + 8'h01;
                end
            end
            else begin
                secs <= secs + 8'h01;
            end
        end
    end

VERILOG CODE:
// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);


    reg [7:0] hh_reg;
    reg [7:0] mm_reg;
    reg [7:0] ss_reg;
    reg pm_reg;

    assign hh = hh_reg;
    assign mm = mm_reg;
    assign ss = ss_reg;
    assign pm = pm_reg;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            hh_reg <= 8'b00010010; // 12 in BCD
            mm_reg <= 8'b00000000; // 00 in BCD
            ss_reg <= 8'b00000000; // 00 in BCD
            pm_reg <= 1'b0;        // 0 for AM
        end else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (ss_reg == 8'b01011001) begin // 59 in BCD
                ss_reg <= 0;

                // Increment minutes
                if (mm_reg == 8'b01011001) begin // 59 in BCD
                    mm_reg <= 0;

                    // Increment hours
                    if (hh_reg == 8'b00010010) begin // 12 in BCD
                        hh_reg <= 8'b00000001; // 1 in BCD
                        pm_reg <= ~pm_reg;    // Toggle AM/PM
                    end else if (hh_reg == 8'b00010001) begin // 11 in BCD
                        hh_reg <= 8'b00010010; // 12 in BCD
                    end else begin
                        hh_reg <= hh_reg + 8'b00000001;
                    end
                end else begin
                    mm_reg <= mm_reg + 8'b00000001;
                end
            end else begin
                ss_reg <= ss_reg + 8'b00000001;
            end
        end
    end

endmodule

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hours, minutes, seconds;
    reg pm_reg;

    always @(posedge clk) begin
        if (reset) begin
            hours <= 8'h12; // 12 in BCD
            minutes <= 8'h00; // 00 in BCD
            seconds <= 8'h00; // 00 in BCD
            pm_reg <= 0; // AM
        end
        else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (seconds == 8'h59) begin
                seconds <= 8'h00;

                // Increment minutes
                if (minutes == 8'h59) begin
                    minutes <= 8'h00;

                    // Increment hours
                    if (hours == 8'h11) begin
                        hours <= 8'h12;
                        pm_reg <= ~pm_reg; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end
                    else if (hours == 8'h12) begin
                        hours <= 8'h01;
                    end
                    else begin
                        hours <= hours + 1;
                    end
                end
                else begin
                    minutes <= minutes + 1;
                end
            end
            else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 1;
            end
        end
    end

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = pm_reg;
endmodule

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

    reg am_pm;

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;

            hours <= 8'h12;  // 12:00 AM
            minutes <= 8'h00;

            am_pm <= 0;  // AM

                    minutes <= 8'h00;

                    end else if (hours == 8'h11) begin
                        hours <= 8'h12;

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hours, minutes, seconds;
    reg pm_reg;

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = pm_reg;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            seconds <= 8'h00;
            minutes <= 8'h00;
            hours <= 8'h12;
            pm_reg <= 1'b0; // AM
        end else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (seconds == 8'h59) begin
                seconds <= 8'h00;
                
                // Increment minutes
                if (minutes == 8'h59) begin
                    minutes <= 8'h00;
                    
                    // Increment hours
                    if (hours == 8'h12) begin
                        hours <= 8'h01;  // Wrap around to 1
                        pm_reg <= ~pm_reg;  // Toggle AM/PM
                    end else begin
                        if (hours == 8'h11) begin
                            hours <= 8'h12;  // Transition from 11 to 12
                        end else begin
                            hours <= hours + 8'h01;
                        end
                    end
                end else begin
                    minutes <= minutes + 8'h01;
                end
            end else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 8'h01;
            end
        end
    end
endmodule

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,

    reg [7:0] hh_reg;
    reg [7:0] mm_reg;
    reg [7:0] ss_reg;

VERILOG CODE:
// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] h_reg, m_reg, s_reg;
    reg pm_reg;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset to 12:00:00 AM
            h_reg <= 8'd12;
            m_reg <= 8'd0;
            s_reg <= 8'd0;
            pm_reg <= 1'b0;
        end
        else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (s_reg == 8'd59) begin
                s_reg <= 8'd0;
                // Increment minutes
                if (m_reg == 8'd59) begin
                    m_reg <= 8'd0;
                    // Increment hours
                    if (h_reg == 8'd12) begin
                        h_reg <= 8'd1;
                        pm_reg <= ~pm_reg; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end
                    else if (h_reg == 8'd11) begin
                        h_reg <= h_reg + 8'd1;
                        pm_reg <= ~pm_reg; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end
                    else begin
                        h_reg <= h_reg + 8'd1;
                    end
                end
                else begin
                    m_reg <= m_reg + 8'd1;
                end
            end
            else begin
                s_reg <= s_reg + 8'd1;
            end
        end
    end

    // Output the clock values
    assign hh = h_reg;
    assign mm = m_reg;
    assign ss = s_reg;
    assign pm = pm_reg;

endmodule

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hours;   // BCD hours (01-12)
    reg [7:0] minutes; // BCD minutes (00-59)
    reg [7:0] seconds; // BCD seconds (00-59)
    reg am_pm;         // AM/PM flag

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = am_pm;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            hours <= 8'h12; // 12 AM
            minutes <= 8'h00;
            seconds <= 8'h00;
            am_pm <= 1'b0;  // AM
        end else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (seconds[3:0] == 4'h9) begin
                seconds[3:0] <= 4'h0;
                if (seconds[7:4] == 4'h5) begin
                    seconds[7:4] <= 4'h0;
                    
                    // Increment minutes
                    if (minutes[3:0] == 4'h9) begin
                        minutes[3:0] <= 4'h0;
                        if (minutes[7:4] == 4'h5) begin
                            minutes[7:4] <= 4'h0;
                            
                            // Increment hours
                            if (hours == 8'h12) begin
                                hours <= 8'h01;
                                am_pm <= ~am_pm; // Toggle AM/PM
                            end else if (hours[3:0] == 4'h9) begin

                                hours[7:4] <= hours[7:4] + 1;

                    seconds[7:4] <= seconds[7:4] + 1;
                end
            end else begin
                seconds[3:0] <= seconds[3:0] + 1;
            end
        end
    end

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] current_hh;
    reg [7:0] current_mm;
    reg [7:0] current_ss;
    reg pm_reg;

    always @(posedge clk) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset the clock to 12:00:00 AM
            current_hh <= 8'h12; // 12 in BCD is 0001 0010
            current_mm <= 8'h00;
            current_ss <= 8'h00;
            pm_reg <= 0; // AM

                if (current_mm == 8'h59) begin
                    current_mm <= 8'h00;

                    // Increment hours

                        current_hh <= 8'h01;

                    end
                end else begin
                    current_mm <= current_mm + 1;
                end
            end else begin
                current_ss <= current_ss + 1;
            end
        end
    end

    // Output assignments
    assign hh = current_hh;
    assign mm = current_mm;
    assign ss = current_ss;
    assign pm = pm_reg;
