VERILOG CODE:
// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

    reg [7:0] hour;
    reg [7:0] minute;
    reg [7:0] second;
    reg is_pm;
    
    assign hh = hour;
    assign mm = minute;
    assign ss = second;
    assign pm = is_pm;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            hour <= 8'h12;  // 12 in BCD (AM)
            minute <= 8'h00;
            second <= 8'h00;
            is_pm <= 1'b0;  // AM
        end else if (ena) begin
            if (second == 8'h59) begin
                second <= 8'h00;
                if (minute == 8'h59) begin
                    minute <= 8'h00;
                    if (hour == 8'h12) begin
                        hour <= 8'h01;
                        is_pm <= ~is_pm;  // Toggle AM/PM
                    end else if (hour == 8'h11) begin
                        hour <= 8'h12;  // Next hour after 11 is 12
                    end else begin
                        hour <= hour + 8'h01;
                    end
                end else begin
                    minute <= minute + 8'h01;
                end
            end else begin
                second <= second + 8'h01;
            end
        end
    end

endmodule

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

    reg [7:0] seconds, minutes, hours;
    reg pm_reg;

    assign ss = seconds;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign hh = hours;
    assign pm = pm_reg;

    always @(posedge clk) begin
        if (reset) begin
            pm_reg <= 0;
            hours <= 8'h12;   // 12:00 AM
            minutes <= 8'h00;
            seconds <= 8'h00;
        end
        else if (ena) begin
            if (seconds == 8'h59) begin
                seconds <= 8'h00;           // Increment minutes
                if (minutes == 8'h59) begin
                    minutes <= 8'h00;       // Increment hours
                    if (hours == 8'h11) begin
                        hours <= 8'h12;
                        pm_reg <= ~pm_reg; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end
                    else if (hours == 8'h12) begin
                        hours <= 8'h01;
                    end
                    else begin
                        hours <= hours + 1;
                    end
                end
                else begin
                    minutes <= minutes + 1;
                end
            end
            else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 1;
            end
        end
    end
endmodule

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

    reg [7:0] hours;
    reg [7:0] minutes;
    reg [7:0] seconds;
    reg pm_reg;
    
    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = pm_reg;
    
    always @(posedge clk) begin
        if (reset) begin
            hours <= 8'b00010010;  // 12 in BCD
            minutes <= 8'b00000000; // 00 in BCD
            seconds <= 8'b00000000; // 00 in BCD
            pm_reg <= 1'b0;          // AM
        end
        else if (ena) begin
            if (seconds == 8'h59) begin
                seconds <= 8'b00000000;
                if (minutes == 8'h59) begin
                    minutes <= 8'b00000000;
                    if (hours == 8'h12) begin
                        hours <= 8'b00000001; // 01 in BCD
                        pm_reg <= ~pm_reg;
                    end
                    else if (hours == 8'h11) begin
                        hours <= 8'b00010010; // 12 in BCD
                    end
                    else begin
                        if (hours[3:0] == 4'h9) begin
                            hours <= {hours[7:4] + 1'b1, 4'b0000};
                        end
                        else begin
                            hours <= hours + 1'b1;
                        end
                    end
                end 
                else begin
                    if (minutes[3:0] == 4'h9) begin
                        minutes <= {minutes[7:4] + 1'b1, 4'b0000};
                    end
                    else begin
                        minutes <= minutes + 1'b1;
                    end
                end
            end 
            else begin
                if (seconds[3:0] == 4'h9) begin
                    seconds <= {seconds[7:4] + 1'b1, 4'b0000};
                end
                else begin
                    seconds <= seconds + 1'b1;
                end
            end
        end
    end

endmodule

Initiating comile/functionality check.
VERILOG CODE:
// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

    reg [5:0] sec, min;
    reg [4:0] hour;
    reg pm_reg;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            sec <= 6'd0;
            min <= 6'd0;
            hour <= 5'd12;
            pm_reg <= 1'b0;
        end else if (ena) begin
            // Seconds counter
            if (sec == 6'd59) begin
                sec <= 6'd0;
                // Minutes counter
                if (min == 6'd59) begin
                    min <= 6'd0;
                    // Hour counter
                    if (hour == 5'd12) begin
                        hour <= 5'd1;
                        pm_reg <= ~pm_reg; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end else begin
                        hour <= hour + 5'd1;
                    end
                end else begin
                    min <= min + 6'd1;
                end
            end else begin
                sec <= sec + 6'd1;
            end
        end
    end

    // Output logic for BCD encoding
    assign ss = {sec[5:4], sec[3:0]};
    assign mm = {min[5:4], min[3:0]};
    assign hh = (hour == 5'd0 || hour > 5'd12) ? 8'd1 : {hour[4:4], hour[3:0]};
    assign pm = pm_reg;

endmodule

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] second_counter;
    reg [7:0] minute_counter;
    reg [7:0] hour_counter;
    reg pm_reg;

    assign ss = second_counter;
    assign mm = minute_counter;
    assign hh = hour_counter;
    assign pm = pm_reg;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            second_counter <= 8'b00000000; // 00 seconds
            minute_counter <= 8'b00000000; // 00 minutes
            hour_counter <= 8'b00010010;   // 12 hours
            pm_reg <= 1'b0; // AM
        end else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (second_counter == 8'b01011001) begin // 59 seconds
                second_counter <= 8'b00000000;
                // Increment minutes
                if (minute_counter == 8'b01011001) begin // 59 minutes
                    minute_counter <= 8'b00000000;
                    // Increment hours
                    if (hour_counter == 8'b00010001) begin // 11 hours
                        hour_counter <= 8'b00010010; // 12 hours
                        pm_reg <= ~pm_reg; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end else if (hour_counter == 8'b00010010) begin // 12 hours
                        hour_counter <= 8'b00000001; // 01 hour
                    end else begin
                        hour_counter <= hour_counter + 1;
                    end
                end else begin
                    minute_counter <= minute_counter + 1;
                end
            end else begin
                second_counter <= second_counter + 1;
            end
        end
    end

endmodule

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

    reg [7:0] hours;
    reg [7:0] minutes;
    reg [7:0] seconds;
    reg pm_reg;

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = pm_reg;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12 in BCD
            minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            pm_reg <= 0; // AM
        end else if (ena) begin
            if (seconds == 8'b0101_1001) begin
                seconds <= 8'b0000_0000;
                if (minutes == 8'b0101_1001) begin
                    minutes <= 8'b0000_0000;
                    if (hours == 8'b0001_0010) begin
                        hours <= 8'b0000_0001; // 1 in BCD
                        pm_reg <= ~pm_reg;
                    end else if (hours == 8'b0000_1001) begin
                        hours <= 8'b0001_0000; // 10 in BCD
                    end else if (hours == 8'b0001_0000) begin
                        hours <= 8'b0001_0001; // 11 in BCD
                    end else if (hours == 8'b0001_0001) begin
                        hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12 in BCD
                    end else begin
                        hours <= hours + 8'b0000_0001;
                    end
                end else begin
                    minutes <= minutes + 8'b0000_0001;
                end
            end else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 8'b0000_0001;
            end
        end
    end

endmodule

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hours;
    reg [7:0] minutes;
    reg [7:0] seconds;
    reg am_pm;

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = am_pm;

    always @(posedge clk) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset to 12:00:00 AM
            hours <= 8'b00010010; // BCD for 12
            minutes <= 8'b00000000; // BCD for 00
            seconds <= 8'b00000000; // BCD for 00
            am_pm <= 0; // AM
        end
        else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (seconds == 8'b01011001) begin // BCD for 59
                seconds <= 8'b00000000;
                // Increment minutes
                if (minutes == 8'b01011001) begin // BCD for 59
                    minutes <= 8'b00000000;
                    // Increment hours
                    if (hours == 8'b00010010) begin // BCD for 12
                        hours <= 8'b00000001; // BCD for 01
                        am_pm <= ~am_pm; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end
                    else if (hours == 8'b00010001) begin // BCD for 11
                        hours <= 8'b00010010; // BCD for 12
                    end
                    else begin
                        if (hours[3:0] == 4'b1001) begin // BCD 9
                            hours[3:0] <= 4'b0000; // Reset lower BCD digit
                            hours[7:4] <= hours[7:4] + 1; // Increment upper BCD digit
                        end
                        else begin
                            hours <= hours + 1;
                        end
                    end
                end
                else begin
                    if (minutes[3:0] == 4'b1001) begin // BCD 9
                        minutes[3:0] <= 4'b0000; // Reset lower BCD digit
                        minutes[7:4] <= minutes[7:4] + 1; // Increment upper BCD digit
                    end
                    else begin
                        minutes <= minutes + 1;
                    end
                end
            end
            else begin
                if (seconds[3:0] == 4'b1001) begin // BCD 9
                    seconds[3:0] <= 4'b0000; // Reset lower BCD digit
                    seconds[7:4] <= seconds[7:4] + 1; // Increment upper BCD digit
                end
                else begin
                    seconds <= seconds + 1;
                end
            end
        end
    end

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

    reg [7:0] hours, minutes, seconds;
    reg am_pm;

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = am_pm;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            hours <= 8'h12;  // 12 in BCD
            minutes <= 8'h00;
            seconds <= 8'h00;
            am_pm <= 1'b0;  // AM
        end
        else if (ena) begin
            if (seconds == 8'h59) begin
                seconds <= 8'h00;
                if (minutes == 8'h59) begin
                    minutes <= 8'h00;
                    if (hours == 8'h12) begin
                        hours <= 8'h01;  // Wrap from 12 to 01
                        am_pm <= ~am_pm; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end
                    else if (hours == 8'h11) begin
                        hours <= 8'h12; // 11 to 12, no toggle AM/PM
                    end
                    else begin
                        hours <= hours + 8'h01;
                    end
                end
                else begin
                    minutes <= minutes + 8'h01;
                end
            end
            else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 8'h01;
            end
        end
    end

endmodule

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

    reg [7:0] hours, minutes, seconds;
    reg am_pm;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12 in BCD
            minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            am_pm <= 0; // AM
        end else if (ena) begin
            if (seconds == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // reset seconds to 00
                if (minutes == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                    minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // reset minutes to 00
                    if (hours == 8'b0001_0010) begin // 12 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0000_0001; // advance hours to 01
                        am_pm <= ~am_pm; // toggle AM/PM
                    end else if (hours == 8'b0001_0001) begin // 11 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // advance hours to 12
                    end else begin
                        hours <= hours + 1; // increment hours
                    end
                end else begin
                    minutes <= minutes + 1; // increment minutes
                end
            end else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 1; // increment seconds
            end
        end
    end

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = am_pm;
    
endmodule

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

    reg [7:0] hours, minutes, seconds;
    reg am_pm; // 0 for AM, 1 for PM
    
    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = am_pm;
    
    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset to 12:00:00 AM
            hours <= 8'h12;
            minutes <= 8'h00;
            seconds <= 8'h00;
            am_pm <= 0;
        end
        else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (seconds == 8'h59) begin
                seconds <= 8'h00;
                // Increment minutes
                if (minutes == 8'h59) begin
                    minutes <= 8'h00;
                    // Increment hours
                    if (hours == 8'h12) begin
                        hours <= 8'h01;
                        am_pm <= ~am_pm; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end
                    else if (hours == 8'h11) begin
                        hours <= 8'h12;
                    end
                    else begin
                        hours <= hours + 8'h01;
                    end
                end
                else begin
                    minutes <= minutes + 8'h01;
                end
            end
            else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 8'h01;
            end
        end
    end

VERILOG CODE:
// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hours;
    reg [7:0] minutes;
    reg [7:0] seconds;
    reg pm_reg;

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = pm_reg;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            hours <= 8'h12; // 12 in BCD
            minutes <= 8'h00;
            seconds <= 8'h00;
            pm_reg <= 1'b0; // AM
        end else if (ena) begin
            // Increment the seconds
            if (seconds == 8'h59) begin
                seconds <= 8'h00;
                // Increment the minutes
                if (minutes == 8'h59) begin
                    minutes <= 8'h00;
                    // Increment the hours
                    if (hours == 8'h12) begin
                        hours <= 8'h01;
                        pm_reg <= ~pm_reg; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end else if (hours == 8'h11) begin
                        hours <= 8'h12; // Go to 12
                    end else begin
                        hours <= hours + 8'h01;
                    end
                end else begin
                    minutes <= minutes + 8'h01;
                end
            end else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 8'h01;
            end
        end
    end
endmodule

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

    reg [7:0] hours;
    reg [7:0] minutes;
    reg [7:0] seconds;
    reg pm_reg;

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = pm_reg;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Resetting the clock to 12:00:00 AM
            hours <= 8'h12;
            minutes <= 8'h00;
            seconds <= 8'h00;
            pm_reg <= 1'b0; // AM
        end else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (seconds == 8'h59) begin
                seconds <= 8'h00;
                // Increment minutes
                if (minutes == 8'h59) begin
                    minutes <= 8'h00;
                    // Increment hours
                    if (hours == 8'h12) begin
                        hours <= 8'h01;
                        pm_reg <= ~pm_reg; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end else if (hours == 8'h11) begin
                        hours <= 8'h12;
                    end else begin
                        hours <= hours + 8'h01;
                    end
                end else begin
                    minutes <= minutes + 8'h01;
                end
            end else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 8'h01;
            end
        end
    end
endmodule

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] sec, min, hour;
    reg pm_reg;

    assign ss = sec;
    assign mm = min;
    assign hh = hour;
    assign pm = pm_reg;

    always @(posedge clk) begin
        if (reset) begin
            sec <= 8'd0;
            min <= 8'd0;
            hour <= 8'd12; // start at 12:00:00 AM
            pm_reg <= 1'b0; // AM
        end else if (ena) begin
            if (sec == 8'd59) begin
                sec <= 8'd0;
                if (min == 8'd59) begin
                    min <= 8'd0;
                    if (hour == 8'd11) begin
                        hour <= 8'd12;
                        pm_reg <= ~pm_reg; // toggle AM/PM
                    end else if (hour == 8'd12) begin
                        hour <= 8'd1;
                    end else begin
                        hour <= hour + 8'd1;
                    end
                end else begin
                    min <= min + 8'd1;
                end
            end else begin
                sec <= sec + 8'd1;
            end
        end
    end
endmodule

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg pm_reg;
    reg [7:0] hh_reg;
    reg [7:0] mm_reg;
    reg [7:0] ss_reg;

    // Assign internal registers to outputs
    assign pm = pm_reg;
    assign hh = hh_reg;
    assign mm = mm_reg;
    assign ss = ss_reg;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // On reset, set the time to 12:00:00 AM
            hh_reg <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12 in BCD
            mm_reg <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            ss_reg <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            pm_reg <= 0; // AM
        end
        else if (ena) begin
            // Increment the seconds
            if (ss_reg == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                ss_reg <= 8'b0000_0000; // Wrap to 00
                // Increment the minutes
                if (mm_reg == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                    mm_reg <= 8'b0000_0000; // Wrap to 00
                    // Increment the hours
                    if (hh_reg == 8'b0001_0010) begin // 12 in BCD
                        hh_reg <= 8'b0000_0001; // Wrap to 01
                        pm_reg <= ~pm_reg; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end 
                    else if (hh_reg == 8'b0001_0001) begin // 11 in BCD
                        hh_reg <= 8'b0001_0010; // Go to 12
                    end
                    else begin
                        // Increment hour normally
                        hh_reg <= hh_reg + 1;
                    end
                end 
                else begin
                    mm_reg <= mm_reg + 1;
                end
            end 
            else begin
                ss_reg <= ss_reg + 1;
            end
        end
    end
endmodule

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

    reg [7:0] hours, minutes, seconds;
    reg am_pm;

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = am_pm;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            hours <= 8'h12; // BCD for 12
            minutes <= 8'h00; // BCD for 00
            seconds <= 8'h00; // BCD for 00
            am_pm <= 1'b0; // 0 for AM
        end

            // Increment seconds

                seconds <= 8'h00;

Initiating comile/functionality check.
VERILOG CODE:
// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hours;
    reg [7:0] minutes;
    reg [7:0] seconds;
    reg pm_reg;

    always @(posedge clk) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset to 12:00:00 AM
            hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12
            minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00
            seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00
            pm_reg <= 0; // AM
        end else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (seconds == 8'b0101_1001) begin
                seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset seconds to 00
                // Increment minutes
                if (minutes == 8'b0101_1001) begin
                    minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset minutes to 00
                    // Increment hours
                    if (hours == 8'b0001_0010) begin
                        hours <= 8'b0000_0001; // Roll over to 01
                    end else if (hours == 8'b0001_0001) begin
                        hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // Advance from 11 to 12
                        pm_reg <= ~pm_reg; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end else begin
                        hours <= hours + 1; // Increment hours normally
                    end
                end else begin
                    minutes <= minutes + 1; // Increment minutes normally
                end
            end else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 1; // Increment seconds normally
            end
        end
    end

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = pm_reg;
endmodule

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

    reg pm_reg;

    assign ss = sec;
    assign mm = min;
    assign hh = hrs;
    assign pm = pm_reg;

    always @(posedge clk) begin
        if (reset) begin
            sec <= 8'h00; // Reset seconds to 00
            min <= 8'h00; // Reset minutes to 00
            hrs <= 8'h12; // Reset hours to 12
            pm_reg <= 0;  // Reset to AM

                    min <= 8'h00;

                    // Increment hours

                        hrs <= 8'h01;
                        pm_reg <= ~pm_reg; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end else if (hrs == 8'h11) begin
                        hrs <= 8'h12; // Transition from 11 to 12
                    end else begin
                        hrs <= hrs + 1;
                    end
                end else begin
                    min <= min + 1;
                end
            end else begin
                sec <= sec + 1;
            end
        end
    end

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hours;
    reg [7:0] minutes;
    reg [7:0] seconds;
    reg pm_reg;
    
    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = pm_reg;
    
    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset time to 12:00:00 AM
            hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12 in BCD
            minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00
            seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00
            pm_reg <= 0; // AM
        end
        else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (seconds == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                seconds <= 8'b0000_0000;
                // Increment minutes
                if (minutes == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                    minutes <= 8'b0000_0000;
                    // Increment hours
                    if (hours == 8'b0001_0010) begin // 12 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0000_0001; // 01 in BCD
                        pm_reg <= ~pm_reg; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end
                    else if (hours == 8'b0001_0001) begin // 11 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12 in BCD
                    end
                    else begin
                        hours <= hours + 8'b0000_0001;
                    end
                end
                else begin
                    minutes <= minutes + 8'b0000_0001;
                end
            end
            else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 8'b0000_0001;
            end
        end
    end
endmodule

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] seconds, minutes, hours;
    reg pm_flag;

    assign ss = seconds;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign hh = hours;
    assign pm = pm_flag;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset the clock to 12:00:00 AM
            seconds <= 8'b0;
            minutes <= 8'b0;
            hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12 in BCD
            pm_flag <= 1'b0; // AM
        end else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (seconds[3:0] == 4'd9) begin
                if (seconds[7:4] == 4'd5) begin
                    seconds <= 8'b0;
                    // Increment minutes
                    if (minutes[3:0] == 4'd9) begin
                        if (minutes[7:4] == 4'd5) begin
                            minutes <= 8'b0;
                            // Increment hours
                            if (hours == 8'b0001_0010) begin // 12
                                hours <= 8'b0_001_0001; // 01 in BCD
                                pm_flag <= ~pm_flag; // Toggle AM/PM
                            end else if (hours == 8'b0000_1001) begin // 09
                                hours <= 8'b0001_0000; // 10
                            end else if (hours[3:0] == 4'd9) begin
                                hours <= {hours[7:4] + 1, 4'd0}; // Move from 09 to 10
                            end else begin
                                hours <= hours + 8'd1;
                            end
                        end else begin
                            minutes <= {minutes[7:4] + 1, 4'd0};
                        end
                    end else begin
                        minutes <= minutes + 8'd1;
                    end
                end else begin
                    seconds <= {seconds[7:4] + 1, 4'd0};
                end
            end else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 8'd1;
            end
        end
    end

endmodule

VERILOG CODE:
// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);


    reg pm_reg; // PM indicator register
    reg [7:0] hours;
    reg [7:0] minutes;
    reg [7:0] seconds;
    
    assign pm = pm_reg;
    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;

    always @(posedge clk) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset to 12:00:00 AM
            hours <= 8'b00010010;  // 12
            minutes <= 8'b00000000; // 00
            seconds <= 8'b00000000; // 00
            pm_reg <= 1'b0;         // AM
        end else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (seconds == 8'b01011001) begin
                seconds <= 8'b00000000;
                // Increment minutes
                if (minutes == 8'b01011001) begin
                    minutes <= 8'b00000000;
                    // Increment hours
                    if (hours == 8'b00010010) begin
                        hours <= 8'b00000001;
                        pm_reg <= ~pm_reg; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end else if (hours == 8'b00010001) begin
                        hours <= 8'b00010010; // 12
                    end else begin
                        hours <= hours + 1;
                    end
                end else begin
                    minutes <= minutes + 1;
                end
            end else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 1;
            end
        end
    end

endmodule

VERILOG CODE:
// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

    reg pm_reg;
    reg [7:0] hh_reg;
    reg [7:0] mm_reg;
    reg [7:0] ss_reg;

    assign pm = pm_reg;
    assign hh = hh_reg;
    assign mm = mm_reg;
    assign ss = ss_reg;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            ss_reg <= 8'h00; // 00 in BCD
            mm_reg <= 8'h00; // 00 in BCD
            hh_reg <= 8'h12; // 12 in BCD
            pm_reg <= 1'b0;  // AM
        end
        else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (ss_reg == 8'h59) begin
                ss_reg <= 8'h00;
                
                // Increment minutes
                if (mm_reg == 8'h59) begin
                    mm_reg <= 8'h00;

                    // Increment hours
                    if (hh_reg == 8'h12) begin
                        hh_reg <= 8'h01;
                        pm_reg <= ~pm_reg;
                    end
                    else if (hh_reg == 8'h11) begin
                        hh_reg <= hh_reg + 1'b1;
                    end
                    else begin
                        hh_reg <= hh_reg + 1'b1;
                    end
                end
                else begin
                    mm_reg <= mm_reg + 1'b1;
                end
            end
            else begin
                ss_reg <= ss_reg + 1'b1;
            end
        end
    end

endmodule

module top_module(

    input reset,

    output pm,

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg pm_reg;
    reg [7:0] hh_reg, mm_reg, ss_reg;
    
    always @(posedge clk) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset to 12:00:00 AM
            hh_reg <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12 in BCD
            mm_reg <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            ss_reg <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            pm_reg <= 1'b0; // 0 for AM
        end else if (ena) begin
            if (ss_reg == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                ss_reg <= 8'b0000_0000;
                
                if (mm_reg == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                    mm_reg <= 8'b0000_0000;

                    if (hh_reg == 8'b0001_0010) begin // 12 in BCD
                        hh_reg <= 8'b0000_0001; // 01 in BCD
                        pm_reg <= ~pm_reg; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end else if (hh_reg == 8'b0001_0001) begin // 11 in BCD
                        hh_reg <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12 in BCD
                    end else begin
                        hh_reg[3:0] <= (hh_reg[3:0] == 4'b1001) ? 4'b0000 : hh_reg[3:0] + 1; // Increment hours
                        if (hh_reg[3:0] == 4'b0000) hh_reg[7:4] <= hh_reg[7:4] + 1; // Handle BCD carry
                    end
                    
                end else begin
                    mm_reg[3:0] <= (mm_reg[3:0] == 4'b1001) ? 4'b0000 : mm_reg[3:0] + 1; // Increment minutes
                    if (mm_reg[3:0] == 4'b0000) mm_reg[7:4] <= mm_reg[7:4] + 1; // Handle BCD carry
                end
                
            end else begin
                ss_reg[3:0] <= (ss_reg[3:0] == 4'b1001) ? 4'b0000 : ss_reg[3:0] + 1; // Increment seconds
                if (ss_reg[3:0] == 4'b0000) ss_reg[7:4] <= ss_reg[7:4] + 1; // Handle BCD carry
            end
        end
    end

    // Assign outputs
    assign hh = hh_reg;
    assign mm = mm_reg;
    assign ss = ss_reg;
    assign pm = pm_reg;

endmodule

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hh_reg;
    reg [7:0] mm_reg;
    reg [7:0] ss_reg;
    reg pm_reg;
    
    assign hh = hh_reg;
    assign mm = mm_reg;
    assign ss = ss_reg;
    assign pm = pm_reg;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset to 12:00:00 AM
            hh_reg <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12 in BCD
            mm_reg <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            ss_reg <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            pm_reg <= 1'b0; // AM
        end
        else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (ss_reg == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                ss_reg <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset seconds to 00
                // Increment minutes
                if (mm_reg == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                    mm_reg <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset minutes to 00
                    // Increment hours
                    if (hh_reg == 8'b0001_0010) begin // 12 in BCD
                        hh_reg <= 8'b0000_0001; // Reset hours to 01
                        pm_reg <= ~pm_reg; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end
                    else if (hh_reg == 8'b0001_0001) begin // 11 in BCD
                        hh_reg <= 8'b0001_0010; // Advance to 12
                    end
                    else begin
                        // Increment hour by one
                        if (hh_reg[3:0] == 4'b1001) begin // If the lower BCD digit is 9
                            hh_reg <= {hh_reg[7:4] + 1'b1, 4'b0000}; // Carry over
                        end
                        else begin
                            hh_reg <= hh_reg + 8'b0000_0001; // Increment lower BCD digit
                        end
                    end
                end
                else begin
                    // Increment minute by one
                    if (mm_reg[3:0] == 4'b1001) begin // If the lower BCD digit is 9
                        mm_reg <= {mm_reg[7:4] + 1'b1, 4'b0000}; // Carry over
                    end
                    else begin
                        mm_reg <= mm_reg + 8'b0000_0001; // Increment lower BCD digit
                    end
                end
            end
            else begin
                // Increment second by one
                if (ss_reg[3:0] == 4'b1001) begin // If the lower BCD digit is 9
                    ss_reg <= {ss_reg[7:4] + 1'b1, 4'b0000}; // Carry over
                end
                else begin
                    ss_reg <= ss_reg + 8'b0000_0001; // Increment lower BCD digit
                end
            end
        end
    end

endmodule

                    else begin
                        // Increment hour by one
                        if (hh_reg[3:0] == 4'b1001) begin // If the lower BCD digit is 9
                            hh_reg <= {hh_reg[7:4] + 1'b1, 4'b0000}; // Carry over
                        end
                        else begin
                            hh_reg <= hh_reg + 8'b0000_0001; // Increment lower BCD digit
                        end
                    end
                end
                else begin
                    // Increment minute by one
                    if (mm_reg[3:0] == 4'b1001) begin // If the lower BCD digit is 9
                        mm_reg <= {mm_reg[7:4] + 1'b1, 4'b0000}; // Carry over
                    end
                    else begin
                        mm_reg <= mm_reg + 8'b0000_0001; // Increment lower BCD digit
                    end
                end
            end
            else begin
                // Increment second by one
                if (ss_reg[3:0] == 4'b1001) begin // If the lower BCD digit is 9
                    ss_reg <= {ss_reg[7:4] + 1'b1, 4'b0000}; // Carry over
                end
                else begin
                    ss_reg <= ss_reg + 8'b0000_0001; // Increment lower BCD digit
                end
            end
        end
    end

endmodule

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hour;
    reg [7:0] min;
    reg [7:0] sec;
    reg pm_reg;

    always @(posedge clk) begin
        if (reset) begin
            hour <= 8'b0001_0010; // BCD for 12
            min <= 8'b0000_0000;  // BCD for 00
            sec <= 8'b0000_0000;  // BCD for 00
            pm_reg <= 0; // AM
        end else if (ena) begin
            if (sec == 8'b0101_1001) begin // BCD for 59
                sec <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset seconds to 00
                if (min == 8'b0101_1001) begin // BCD for 59
                    min <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset minutes to 00
                    if (hour == 8'b0001_0010) begin // If hour is 12
                        hour <= 8'b0000_0001; // BCD for 01
                        pm_reg <= ~pm_reg; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end else if (hour == 8'b0001_0001) begin // If hour is 11
                        hour <= 8'b0001_0010; // BCD for 12
                    end else begin
                        hour[3:0] <= (hour[3:0] == 9) ? 4'b0000 : hour[3:0] + 1;
                        if (hour[3:0] == 4'b0000) begin // Reset lower BCD digit if it wraps around
                            hour[7:4] <= hour[7:4] + 1;
                        end
                    end
                end else begin
                    min[3:0] <= (min[3:0] == 9) ? 4'b0000 : min[3:0] + 1;
                    if (min[3:0] == 4'b0000) begin // Reset lower BCD digit if it wraps around
                        min[7:4] <= min[7:4] + 1;
                    end
                end
            end else begin
                sec[3:0] <= (sec[3:0] == 9) ? 4'b0000 : sec[3:0] + 1;
                if (sec[3:0] == 4'b0000) begin // Reset lower BCD digit if it wraps around
                    sec[7:4] <= sec[7:4] + 1;
                end
            end
        end
    end

    assign hh = hour;
    assign mm = min;
    assign ss = sec;
    assign pm = pm_reg;

module top_module(

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hours;   // BCD hours
    reg [7:0] minutes; // BCD minutes
    reg [7:0] seconds; // BCD seconds
    reg am_pm;         // AM/PM indicator

    always @(posedge clk) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset the time to 12:00:00 AM
            hours <= 8'b0001_0010;  // 12 in BCD
            minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            am_pm <= 0; // AM
        end
        else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (seconds == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // Wrap to 00
                // Increment minutes
                if (minutes == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                    minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // Wrap to 00
                    // Increment hours
                    if (hours == 8'b0001_0010) begin // 12 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0000_0001; // Wrap to 01
                        am_pm <= ~am_pm; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end
                    else if (hours == 8'b0001_0001) begin // 11 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // Go to 12
                    end
                    else begin
                        if (hours[3:0] == 4'b1001) begin // If ones digit is 9
                            hours <= {hours[7:4] + 1, 4'b0000}; // Increment tens digit and reset ones
                        end
                        else begin
                            hours <= hours + 1; // Normal increment
                        end
                    end
                end
                else begin
                    if (minutes[3:0] == 4'b1001) begin // If ones digit is 9
                        minutes <= {minutes[7:4] + 1, 4'b0000}; // Increment tens digit and reset ones
                    end
                    else begin
                        minutes <= minutes + 1; // Normal increment
                    end
                end
            end
            else begin
                if (seconds[3:0] == 4'b1001) begin // If ones digit is 9
                    seconds <= {seconds[7:4] + 1, 4'b0000}; // Increment tens digit and reset ones
                end
                else begin
                    seconds <= seconds + 1; // Normal increment
                end
            end
        end
    end

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = am_pm;

endmodule

                        minutes <= minutes + 1; // Normal increment
                    end
                end
            end
            else begin
                if (seconds[3:0] == 4'b1001) begin // If ones digit is 9
                    seconds <= {seconds[7:4] + 1, 4'b0000}; // Increment tens digit and reset ones
                end
                else begin
                    seconds <= seconds + 1; // Normal increment
                end
            end
        end
    end

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = am_pm;

endmodule

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hours, minutes, seconds;
    reg am_pm;

    // Assign outputs
    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = am_pm;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset condition
            seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            hours <= 8'b0001_0010;   // 12 in BCD
            am_pm <= 0;              // AM
        end else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (seconds[3:0] == 4'd9) begin
                if (seconds[7:4] == 4'd5) begin
                    seconds <= 8'b0000_0000;
                    // Increment minutes
                    if (minutes[3:0] == 4'd9) begin
                        if (minutes[7:4] == 4'd5) begin
                            minutes <= 8'b0000_0000;
                            // Increment hours
                            if (hours[3:0] == 4'd9) begin
                                hours[3:0] <= 4'd0;
                                hours[7:4] <= hours[7:4] + 1;
                            end else if ((hours == 8'b0001_0010) && (hours[3:0] == 4'd9)) begin
                                hours <= 8'b0001_0001; // Roll over to 01
                                am_pm <= ~am_pm;       // Toggle AM/PM
                            end else begin
                                hours <= hours + 1;
                            end
                        end else begin
                            minutes[3:0] <= 4'd0;
                            minutes[7:4] <= minutes[7:4] + 1;
                        end
                    end else begin
                        minutes <= minutes + 1;
                    end
                end else begin
                    seconds[3:0] <= 4'd0;
                    seconds[7:4] <= seconds[7:4] + 1;
                end
            end else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 1;
            end
        end
    end
endmodule

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);


    reg [3:0] hours_tens, hours_units;
    reg [3:0] minutes_tens, minutes_units;
    reg [3:0] seconds_tens, seconds_units;
    reg pm_reg;
    
    assign hh = {hours_tens, hours_units};
    assign mm = {minutes_tens, minutes_units};
    assign ss = {seconds_tens, seconds_units};
    assign pm = pm_reg;

    always @(posedge clk) begin
        if (reset) begin
            hours_tens <= 4'd1;
            hours_units <= 4'd2;
            minutes_tens <= 4'd0;
            minutes_units <= 4'd0;
            seconds_tens <= 4'd0;
            seconds_units <= 4'd0;
            pm_reg <= 0; // AM
        end
        else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (seconds_units == 4'd9) begin
                seconds_units <= 4'd0;
                if (seconds_tens == 4'd5) begin
                    seconds_tens <= 4'd0;
                    // Increment minutes
                    if (minutes_units == 4'd9) begin
                        minutes_units <= 4'd0;
                        if (minutes_tens == 4'd5) begin
                            minutes_tens <= 4'd0;
                            // Increment hours
                            if ({hours_tens, hours_units} == 8'd11) begin
                                hours_tens <= 4'd1;
                                hours_units <= 4'd2;
                                pm_reg <= ~pm_reg;
                            end else if ({hours_tens, hours_units} == 8'd12) begin
                                hours_tens <= 4'd0;
                                hours_units <= 4'd1;
                            end else if (hours_units == 4'd9) begin
                                hours_units <= 4'd0;
                                hours_tens <= hours_tens + 1;
                            end else begin
                                hours_units <= hours_units + 1;
                            end
                        end else begin
                            minutes_tens <= minutes_tens + 1;
                        end
                    end else begin
                        minutes_units <= minutes_units + 1;
                    end
                end else begin
                    seconds_tens <= seconds_tens + 1;
                end
            end else begin
                seconds_units <= seconds_units + 1;
            end
        end
    end

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hours, minutes, seconds;
    reg pm_reg;

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = pm_reg;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            hours <= 8'h12; // 12
            minutes <= 8'h00; // 00
            seconds <= 8'h00; // 00
            pm_reg <= 1'b0;  // AM
        end else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (seconds == 8'h59) begin
                seconds <= 8'h00; // Reset seconds
                // Increment minutes
                if (minutes == 8'h59) begin
                    minutes <= 8'h00; // Reset minutes
                    // Increment hours
                    if (hours == 8'h12) begin
                        hours <= 8'h01; // Wrap around to 1
                        // Toggle am/pm
                        pm_reg <= ~pm_reg;
                    end else if (hours == 8'h11) begin
                        hours <= 8'h12; // Next hour is 12
                    end else begin
                        hours <= hours + 8'h01; // Regular increment
                    end
                end else begin
                    minutes <= minutes + 8'h01; // Regular increment
                end
            end else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 8'h01; // Regular increment
            end
        end
    end

endmodule

VERILOG CODE:
// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

    reg [7:0] seconds;
    reg [7:0] minutes;
    reg [7:0] hours;
    reg is_pm;

    always @(posedge clk) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset to 12:00:00 AM
            seconds <= 8'h00;
            minutes <= 8'h00;
            hours <= 8'h12;
            is_pm <= 1'b0;
        end
        else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (seconds == 8'h59) begin
                seconds <= 8'h00;
                // Increment minutes
                if (minutes == 8'h59) begin
                    minutes <= 8'h00;
                    // Increment hours
                    if (hours == 8'h12) begin
                        hours <= 8'h01;
                        is_pm <= ~is_pm; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end
                    else if (hours == 8'h11) begin
                        hours <= 8'h12;
                    end
                    else begin
                        hours <= hours + 1'b1;
                    end
                end
                else begin
                    minutes <= minutes + 1'b1;
                end
            end
            else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 1'b1;
            end
        end
    end

    assign ss = seconds;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign hh = hours;
    assign pm = is_pm;

endmodule

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

    reg [7:0] minutes;
    reg [7:0] seconds;

    assign mm = minutes;

                    end

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hours, mins, secs;
    reg pm_reg;

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = mins;
    assign ss = secs;
    assign pm = pm_reg;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            hours <= 8'b00010010;  // 12:00:00
            mins  <= 8'b00000000;
            secs  <= 8'b00000000;
            pm_reg <= 0;           // AM
        end else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (secs == 8'b01011001) begin
                secs <= 8'b00000000;
                // Increment minutes
                if (mins == 8'b01011001) begin
                    mins <= 8'b00000000;
                    // Increment hours
                    if (hours == 8'b00010010) begin
                        hours <= 8'b00000001; // 1
                    end else if (hours == 8'b00010001) begin
                        hours <= 8'b00010010; // 12
                        pm_reg <= ~pm_reg; // Flip AM/PM
                    end else begin
                        hours <= hours + 8'b00000001;
                    end
                end else begin
                    mins <= mins + 8'b00000001;
                end
            end else begin
                secs <= secs + 8'b00000001;
            end
        end
    end
endmodule

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hh_reg;
    reg [7:0] mm_reg;
    reg [7:0] ss_reg;
    reg pm_reg;

    assign hh = hh_reg;
    assign mm = mm_reg;
    assign ss = ss_reg;
    assign pm = pm_reg;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset to 12:00:00 AM
            hh_reg <= 8'h12;
            mm_reg <= 8'h00;
            ss_reg <= 8'h00;
            pm_reg <= 1'b0;
        end else if (ena) begin

            if (ss_reg == 8'h59) begin
                ss_reg <= 8'h00;
                // Increment the minute counter

                    mm_reg <= 8'h00;

                    if (hh_reg == 8'h12) begin
                        hh_reg <= 8'h01;
                        pm_reg <= ~pm_reg; // Toggle am/pm

                        hh_reg <= 8'h12;
                    end else begin
                        hh_reg <= hh_reg + 8'h01;
                    end
                end else begin
                    mm_reg <= mm_reg + 8'h01;
                end
            end else begin
                ss_reg <= ss_reg + 8'h01;
            end
        end
    end

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hours, minutes, seconds;
    reg am_pm;

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = am_pm;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            hours <= 8'b00010010;    // 12 in BCD
            minutes <= 8'b00000000;  // 00 in BCD
            seconds <= 8'b00000000;  // 00 in BCD
            am_pm <= 0;              // AM
        end else if (ena) begin
            if (seconds == 8'b01011001) begin  // 59 in BCD
                seconds <= 8'b00000000;       // reset to 00
                if (minutes == 8'b01011001) begin  // 59 in BCD
                    minutes <= 8'b00000000;   // reset to 00
                    if (hours == 8'b00010010) begin  // 12 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b00000001;  // reset to 01
                        am_pm <= ~am_pm;      // toggle AM/PM
                    end else if (hours == 8'b00001001) begin  // 09 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b00010000; // advance to 10
                    end else if (hours == 8'b00010001) begin  // 11 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b00010010; // advance to 12
                    end else begin
                        hours <= hours + 1;   // increment hour
                    end
                end else begin
                    if (minutes[3:0] == 4'b1001) begin  // check BCD unit digit
                        minutes <= {minutes[7:4] + 1, 4'b0000};  // increment tens digit
                    end else begin
                        minutes <= minutes + 1;  // increment minute
                    end
                end
            end else begin
                if (seconds[3:0] == 4'b1001) begin  // check BCD unit digit
                    seconds <= {seconds[7:4] + 1, 4'b0000}; // increment tens digit
                end else begin
                    seconds <= seconds + 1;  // increment second
                end
            end
        end

VERILOG CODE:
// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

    reg [7:0] r_hh, r_mm, r_ss;
    reg r_pm;

    assign hh = r_hh;
    assign mm = r_mm;
    assign ss = r_ss;
    assign pm = r_pm;

    always @(posedge clk) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset to 12:00:00 AM
            r_hh <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12 in BCD
            r_mm <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            r_ss <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00 in BCD
            r_pm <= 1'b0;         // AM
        end
        else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (r_ss == 8'b0101_1001) begin
                r_ss <= 8'b0000_0000; // wrap to 00
                // Increment minutes
                if (r_mm == 8'b0101_1001) begin
                    r_mm <= 8'b0000_0000; // wrap to 00
                    // Increment hours
                    if (r_hh == 8'b0001_0010) begin // 12 in BCD
                        r_hh <= 8'b0000_0001; // wrap to 01
                        r_pm <= ~r_pm;       // Toggle AM/PM
                    end
                    else if (r_hh == 8'b0000_1001) begin // 09 in BCD
                        r_hh <= 8'b0001_0000; // 10 in BCD
                    end
                    else if (r_hh == 8'b0001_0000) begin // 10 in BCD
                        r_hh <= 8'b0001_0001; // 11 in BCD
                    end
                    else if (r_hh == 8'b0001_0001) begin // 11 in BCD
                        r_hh <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12 in BCD
                    end
                    else begin
                        r_hh <= r_hh + 1; // Increment hours in BCD
                    end
                end
                else begin
                    r_mm <= r_mm + 1; // Increment minutes
                end
            end
            else begin
                r_ss <= r_ss + 1; // Increment seconds
            end
        end
    end

endmodule
