// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hh_reg, mm_reg, ss_reg;
    reg pm_reg;

    always @(posedge clk) begin
        if (reset) begin
            hh_reg <= 8'h12; // 12 in BCD
            mm_reg <= 8'h00; // 00 in BCD
            ss_reg <= 8'h00; // 00 in BCD
            pm_reg <= 1'b0;  // AM
        end else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (ss_reg == 8'h59) begin
                ss_reg <= 8'h00;
                // Increment minutes
                if (mm_reg == 8'h59) begin
                    mm_reg <= 8'h00;
                    // Increment hours
                    if (hh_reg == 8'h12) begin
                        hh_reg <= 8'h01;
                        pm_reg <= ~pm_reg; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end else if (hh_reg == 8'h11) begin
                        hh_reg <= 8'h12;
                    end else begin
                        hh_reg <= hh_reg + 1'b1;
                    end
                end else begin
                    mm_reg <= mm_reg + 1'b1;
                end
            end else begin
                ss_reg <= ss_reg + 1'b1;
            end
        end
    end

    assign hh = hh_reg;
    assign mm = mm_reg;
    assign ss = ss_reg;
    assign pm = pm_reg;

endmodule

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

    reg [7:0] hours, minutes, seconds;
    reg pm_reg;

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = pm_reg;

    always @(posedge clk) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset the time to 12:00:00 AM
            hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12 in BCD
            minutes <= 8'b0000_0000;
            seconds <= 8'b0000_0000;
            pm_reg <= 1'b0; // AM
        end
        else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (seconds == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                seconds <= 8'b0000_0000;
                // Increment minutes
                if (minutes == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59 in BCD
                    minutes <= 8'b0000_0000;
                    // Increment hours
                    if (hours == 8'b0001_0010) begin // 12 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0000_0001; // 1 in BCD
                        pm_reg <= ~pm_reg; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end
                    else if (hours == 8'b0001_0001) begin // 11 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12 in BCD
                    end
                    else begin
                        hours <= hours + 8'b0000_0001; // Increment hours
                    end
                end
                else begin
                    minutes <= minutes + 8'b0000_0001; // Increment minutes
                end
            end
            else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 8'b0000_0001; // Increment seconds
            end
        end
    end

endmodule

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);


    reg [7:0] hours, minutes, seconds;
    reg am_pm;

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = am_pm;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset to 12:00:00 AM
            hours <= 8'd12;
            minutes <= 8'd0;
            seconds <= 8'd0;
            am_pm <= 1'b0; // AM
        end else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (seconds == 8'd59) begin
                seconds <= 8'd0;
                // Increment minutes
                if (minutes == 8'd59) begin
                    minutes <= 8'd0;
                    // Increment hours
                    if (hours == 8'd12) begin
                        hours <= 8'd1;
                        am_pm <= ~am_pm; // Toggle AM/PM at hour 12 rollover
                    end else if (hours == 8'd11) begin
                        hours <= 8'd12;
                    end else begin
                        hours <= hours + 8'd1;
                    end
                end else begin
                    minutes <= minutes + 8'd1;
                end
            end else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 8'd1;
            end
        end
    end

endmodule

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hours, minutes, seconds;
    reg pm_reg;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset time to 12:00:00 AM
            hours <= 8'h12;   // 12 in BCD
            minutes <= 8'h00; // 00 minutes
            seconds <= 8'h00; // 00 seconds
            pm_reg <= 0;      // AM
        end else if (ena) begin
            // Increment the seconds
            if (seconds == 8'h59) begin
                seconds <= 8'h00;
                // Increment the minutes
                if (minutes == 8'h59) begin
                    minutes <= 8'h00;
                    // Increment the hours
                    if (hours == 8'h12) begin
                        hours <= 8'h01;
                        pm_reg <= ~pm_reg; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end else if (hours == 8'h11) begin
                        hours <= 8'h12;
                    end else begin
                        hours <= hours + 8'h01;
                    end
                end else begin
                    minutes <= minutes + 8'h01;
                end
            end else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 8'h01;
            end
        end
    end

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = pm_reg;

endmodule

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

    
    reg pm_reg;
    reg [7:0] hours, minutes, seconds;

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = pm_reg;

    always @(posedge clk) begin
        if (reset) begin
            // Reset to 12:00:00 AM
            hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // 12
            minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00
            seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // 00
            pm_reg <= 0; // AM
        end else if (ena) begin
            if (seconds == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59
                seconds <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset seconds to 00
                if (minutes == 8'b0101_1001) begin // 59
                    minutes <= 8'b0000_0000; // Reset minutes to 00
                    if (hours == 8'b0001_0010) begin // 12
                        hours <= 8'b0000_0001; // Set hours to 01
                        pm_reg <= ~pm_reg; // Toggle am/pm
                    end else if (hours == 8'b0001_0001) begin // 11
                        hours <= 8'b0001_0010; // Set hours to 12
                    end else begin
                        hours <= hours + 1;
                    end
                end else begin
                    minutes <= minutes + 1;
                end
            end else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 1;
            end
        end
    end
    
endmodule

Initiating comile/functionality check.
VERILOG CODE:
// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hours, minutes, seconds;
    reg _pm;

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = _pm;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            hours <= 8'b0001_0010;  // 12 in BCD
            minutes <= 8'b0000_0000;  // 00 in BCD
            seconds <= 8'b0000_0000;  // 00 in BCD
            _pm <= 1'b0;  // AM
        end
        else if (ena) begin
            if (seconds == 8'b0101_1001) begin  // 59 in BCD
                seconds <= 8'b0000_0000;  // reset to 00
                if (minutes == 8'b0101_1001) begin  // 59 in BCD
                    minutes <= 8'b0000_0000;  // reset to 00
                    if (hours == 8'b0001_0010) begin  // 12 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0000_0001;  // reset to 01
                        _pm <= ~_pm;  // toggle AM/PM
                    end
                    else if (hours == 8'b0001_0001) begin  // 11 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b0001_0010;  // increment to 12
                    end
                    else begin
                        hours <= hours + 1;  // increment hour
                    end
                end
                else begin
                    minutes <= minutes + 1;  // increment minute
                end
            end
            else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 1;  // increment second
            end
        end
    end

endmodule

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hours, minutes, seconds;
    reg am_pm;

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = am_pm;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            hours <= 8'h12;    // Reset to 12:00:00
            minutes <= 8'h00;
            seconds <= 8'h00;
            am_pm <= 1'b0;     // AM
        end else if (ena) begin
            if (seconds == 8'h59) begin
                seconds <= 8'h00;
                if (minutes == 8'h59) begin
                    minutes <= 8'h00;
                    if (hours == 8'h12) begin
                        hours <= 8'h01;
                        am_pm <= ~am_pm;  // Toggle AM/PM
                    end else if (hours == 8'h11) begin
                        hours <= 8'h12;
                    end else begin
                        hours <= hours + 1;
                    end
                end else begin
                    minutes <= minutes + 1;
                end
            end else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 1;
            end
        end
    end
endmodule

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hours, minutes, seconds;
    reg pm_reg;

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = pm_reg;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            hours <= 8'b00010010;  // 12 in BCD
            minutes <= 8'b00000000; // 00 in BCD
            seconds <= 8'b00000000; // 00 in BCD
            pm_reg <= 1'b0;         // AM
        end else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (seconds == 8'b01011001) begin // 59 in BCD
                seconds <= 8'b00000000; // reset to 00

                // Increment minutes
                if (minutes == 8'b01011001) begin // 59 in BCD
                    minutes <= 8'b00000000; // reset to 00

                    // Increment hours
                    if (hours == 8'b00010010) begin // 12 in BCD
                        hours <= 8'b00000001; // set to 01
                        pm_reg <= ~pm_reg;    // toggle am/pm
                    end else if (hours == 8'b00010001 && pm_reg == 1'b1) begin // 11 in BCD and PM
                        hours <= 8'b00010010; // set to 12
                    end else begin
                        hours <= hours + 8'b00000001; // increment hours
                    end
                end else begin
                    minutes <= minutes + 8'b00000001; // increment minutes
                end
            end else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 8'b00000001; // increment seconds
            end
        end
    end

endmodule

// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,

VERILOG CODE:
// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hours;
    reg [7:0] minutes;
    reg [7:0] seconds;
    reg am_pm;

    assign hh = hours;
    assign mm = minutes;
    assign ss = seconds;
    assign pm = am_pm;

    always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
        if (reset) begin
            hours <= 8'd12;  // Reset to 12:00 AM
            minutes <= 8'd0;
            seconds <= 8'd0;
            am_pm <= 0; // AM
        end else if (ena) begin
            if (seconds == 8'd59) begin
                seconds <= 8'd0;
                if (minutes == 8'd59) begin
                    minutes <= 8'd0;
                    if (hours == 8'd12) begin
                        hours <= 8'd1;
                        am_pm <= ~am_pm;  // Toggle AM/PM
                    end else if (hours == 8'd11) begin
                        hours <= hours + 8'd1;  // Increment to 12
                    end else begin
                        hours <= hours + 8'd1;
                    end
                end else begin
                    minutes <= minutes + 8'd1;
                end
            end else begin
                seconds <= seconds + 8'd1;
            end
        end
    end

endmodule

VERILOG CODE:
// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);

reg [7:0] hh_reg, mm_reg, ss_reg;
    reg pm_reg;

    always @(posedge clk) begin
        if (reset) begin
            hh_reg <= 8'h12;     // 12
            mm_reg <= 8'h00;     // 00
            ss_reg <= 8'h00;     // 00
            pm_reg <= 1'b0;      // AM
        end else if (ena) begin
            // Increment seconds
            if (ss_reg == 8'h59) begin
                ss_reg <= 8'h00;

                // Increment minutes
                if (mm_reg == 8'h59) begin
                    mm_reg <= 8'h00;

                    // Increment hours
                    if (hh_reg == 8'h12) begin
                        hh_reg <= 8'h01;
                        pm_reg <= ~pm_reg; // Toggle AM/PM
                    end else if (hh_reg == 8'h11) begin
                        hh_reg <= 8'h12;   // 11 -> 12
                    end else begin
                        hh_reg <= hh_reg + 1'b1;
                    end
                end else begin
                    mm_reg <= mm_reg + 1'b1;
                end
            end else begin
                ss_reg <= ss_reg + 1'b1;
            end
        end
    end

    assign hh = hh_reg;
    assign mm = mm_reg;
    assign ss = ss_reg;
    assign pm = pm_reg;
endmodule

VERILOG CODE:
// Create a set of counters suitable for use as a 12-hour clock (with am/pm indicator). Your counters are clocked by a fast-running clk, with a pulse on ena whenever your clock should increment (i.e., once per second).

// reset resets the clock to 12:00 AM. pm is 0 for AM and 1 for PM. hh, mm, and ss are two BCD (Binary-Coded Decimal) digits each for hours (01-12), minutes (00-59), and seconds (00-59). Reset has higher priority than enable, and can occur even when not enabled.

// Hint: Note that 11:59:59 PM advances to 12:00:00 AM, and 12:59:59 PM advances to 01:00:00 PM. There is no 00:00:00.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,
    input ena,
    output pm,
    output [7:0] hh,
    output [7:0] mm,
    output [7:0] ss);


    reg [7:0] hour;
    reg [7:0] minute;
    reg [7:0] second;
    reg pm_reg;

    assign hh = hour;
    assign mm = minute;
    assign ss = second;
    assign pm = pm_reg;

    always @(posedge clk) begin
        if (reset) begin
            hour <= 8'b00010010;  // 12 in BCD
            minute <= 8'b00000000; // 00 in BCD
            second <= 8'b00000000; // 00 in BCD
            pm_reg <= 0;           // AM
        end else if (ena) begin
            if (second == 8'b01011001) begin  // 59 in BCD
                second <= 8'b00000000;        // reset seconds
                if (minute == 8'b01011001) begin // 59 in BCD
                    minute <= 8'b00000000;       // reset minutes
                    if (hour == 8'b00010010) begin // 12 in BCD
                        hour <= 8'b00000001;       // rollover hour to 01
                        pm_reg <= ~pm_reg;         // toggle AM/PM
                    end else if (hour == 8'b00001001) begin // 9 in BCD
                        hour <= 8'b00010000;       // switch to 10 in BCD
                    end else if (hour == 8'b00010000) begin // 10 in BCD
                        hour <= 8'b00010001;       // switch to 11 in BCD
                    end else begin
                        hour <= hour + 1;
                    end
                end else begin
                    minute <= minute + 1;
                end
            end else begin
                second <= second + 1;
            end
        end
    end

endmodule
